# M03-06 — Chart.js Integration

Integrate Chart.js for visual analytics: 1) Install chart.js and react-chartjs-2. 2) Create ChartCard component supporting: line (trends), bar (comparisons), doughnut (breakdowns). 3) Sales trend chart: daily revenue for selected period with previous period overlay. 4) Comparison bar chart: this period vs last period metrics. 5) Category breakdown doughnut: revenue by product category. 6) Responsive sizing within Command Deck modal. 7) Dark/light mode color schemes (automatic switching). 8) Interactive tooltips with formatted currency values. 9) Chart export button (PNG download). 10) Accessibility: include data table alternative for screen readers. Acceptance Criteria: Charts render within 200ms, update smoothly on period change, colors pass WCAG contrast requirements in both themes, exported images are high quality (2x resolution).

@@ -17,2 +43,88 @@
 
+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};
+
+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {
+  if (theme === 'light') {
+    return {
+      text: '#0f172a',
+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    text: '#e2e8f0',
+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',
+    tooltipBg: '#0f172a',
+    tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.4)',
+    tooltipText: '#e2e8f0',
+    canvas: '#0b1220',
+  };
+};
+
 export default function ChartCard({

+      },

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};
+
+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {
+  if (theme === 'light') {
+    return {
+      text: '#0f172a',
+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    text: '#e2e8f0',
+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',
+    tooltipBg: '#0f172a',
+    tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.4)',
+    tooltipText: '#e2e8f0',
+    canvas: '#0b1220',
+  };
+};

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};
+
+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {
+  if (theme === 'light') {
+    return {
+      text: '#0f172a',
+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    text: '#e2e8f0',
+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',
+    tooltipBg: '#0f172a',
+    tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.4)',
+    tooltipText: '#e2e8f0',
+    canvas: '#0b1220',
+  };
+};

+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });

+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');

+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };

+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);

+

+    () => [

+        id: 'agentwpChartBackground',

+        },
+      },

+

+            usePointStyle: true,

+    }
+  };
+

+        : exportLabel;

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};
+
+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {

+                {table.headers.map((header) => (
+                  <th key={header} scope="col">
+                    {header}
+                  </th>
+                ))}

+            </thead>

+              {table.rows.map((row) => (

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,

+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+

+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    text: '#e2e8f0',
+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',
+    tooltipBg: '#0f172a',
+    tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.4)',
+    tooltipText: '#e2e8f0',

+          titleColor: palette.tooltipText,

+      link.href = dataUrl;
+      link.download = exportFilename;
+      document.body.appendChild(link);
+      link.click();

+        window.clearTimeout(exportTimerRef.current);

+      exportTimerRef.current = window.setTimeout(() => {
+        setExportStatus('idle');
+      }, 2000);
+    } catch (error) {
+      setExportStatus('idle');
+    }
+  };
+
+  const resolvedExportLabel =
+    exportStatus === 'exporting'
+      ? 'Exporting...'
+      : exportStatus === 'exported'
+        ? 'Exported'
+        : exportLabel;

+const buildRevenueSeries = (days, base, trend, variance, phase = 0) =>

+    Math.round(base + index * trend + Math.sin(index * 0.45 + phase) * variance)

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;
+};

+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {
+  if (theme === 'light') {
+    return {
+      text: '#0f172a',
+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    text: '#e2e8f0',
+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',
+    tooltipBg: '#0f172a',
+    tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.4)',
+    tooltipText: '#e2e8f0',
+    canvas: '#0b1220',
+  };
+};
+
 export default function ChartCard({
   title = 'Performance snapshot',
   subtitle,
   metric,
   trend,
-  chart,
   footer,
-  theme = 'dark',
+  theme = 'auto',
+  type = 'line',
+  data,
+  options,
+  meta,
+  table,
+  height = 220,
+  exportFilename = 'agentwp-chart.png',
+  exportLabel = 'Export PNG',
+  valueFormatter = formatCurrency,
+  yAxisFormatter,
+  className = '',
 }) {
+  const prefersDark = usePrefersDark();
+  const resolvedTheme = theme === 'auto' ? (prefersDark ? 'dark' : 'light') : theme;
+  const palette = useMemo(() => buildChartPalette(resolvedTheme), [resolvedTheme]);
+  const ChartComponent = CHART_COMPONENTS[type] || Line;
+  const chartRef = useRef(null);
+  const exportTimerRef = useRef(null);
+  const [exportStatus, setExportStatus] = useState('idle');
+  const tableId = useId();
+  const chartId = useId();
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    return () => {
+      if (exportTimerRef.current) {
+        window.clearTimeout(exportTimerRef.current);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  const chartPlugins = useMemo(
+    () => [
+      {
+        id: 'agentwpChartBackground',
+        beforeDraw: (chartInstance) => {
+          const { ctx, width, height } = chartInstance;
+          ctx.save();
+          ctx.fillStyle = palette.canvas;
+          ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
+          ctx.restore();
+        },
+      },
+    ],
+    [palette.canvas]
+  );
+
+  const tooltipCallbacks = useMemo(
+    () => ({
+      label: (context) => {
+        const label = context.dataset?.label ? `${context.dataset.label}: ` : '';
+        const value = resolveTooltipValue(context);
+        return `${label}${valueFormatter(value)}`;
+      },
+    }),
+    [valueFormatter]
+  );
+
+  const mergedOptions = useMemo(() => {
+    const hasScales = type !== 'doughnut';
+    const baseOptions = {
+      responsive: true,
+      maintainAspectRatio: false,
+      devicePixelRatio: 2,
+      animation: {
+        duration: 280,
+        easing: 'easeOutQuart',
+      },
+      interaction: {
+        mode: 'index',
+        intersect: false,
+      },
+      plugins: {
+        legend: {
+          labels: {
+            color: palette.text,
+            font: {
+              family: '"Space Grotesk", "Manrope", system-ui, sans-serif',
+              size: 11,
+              weight: 500,
+            },
+            usePointStyle: true,
+            boxWidth: 8,
+          },
+        },
+        tooltip: {
+          backgroundColor: palette.tooltipBg,
+          borderColor: palette.tooltipBorder,
+          borderWidth: 1,
+          titleColor: palette.tooltipText,
+          bodyColor: palette.tooltipText,
+          callbacks: tooltipCallbacks,
+        },
+      },
+      scales: hasScales
+        ? {
+            x: {
+              ticks: {
+                color: palette.muted,
+              },
+              grid: {
+                color: palette.grid,
+              },
+            },
+            y: {
+              ticks: {
+                color: palette.muted,
+                callback: yAxisFormatter || valueFormatter,
+              },
+              grid: {
+                color: palette.grid,
+              },
+            },
+          }
+        : undefined,
+    };
+
+    if (!options) {
+      return baseOptions;
+    }
+
+    return {
+      ...baseOptions,
+      ...options,
+      plugins: {
+        ...baseOptions.plugins,
+        ...options.plugins,
+        legend: {
+          ...baseOptions.plugins?.legend,
+          ...options.plugins?.legend,
+          labels: {
+            ...baseOptions.plugins?.legend?.labels,
+            ...options.plugins?.legend?.labels,
+          },
+        },
+        tooltip: {
+          ...baseOptions.plugins?.tooltip,
+          ...options.plugins?.tooltip,
+          callbacks: {
+            ...baseOptions.plugins?.tooltip?.callbacks,
+            ...options.plugins?.tooltip?.callbacks,
+          },
+        },
+      },
+      scales: hasScales
+        ? {
+            ...baseOptions.scales,
+            ...options.scales,
+            x: {
+              ...baseOptions.scales?.x,
+              ...options.scales?.x,
+            },
+            y: {
+              ...baseOptions.scales?.y,
+              ...options.scales?.y,
+            },
+          }
+        : options.scales,
+    };
+  }, [options, palette, tooltipCallbacks, type, valueFormatter, yAxisFormatter]);
+
+  const handleExport = () => {
+    if (!chartRef.current || exportStatus === 'exporting') {
+      return;
+    }
+    setExportStatus('exporting');
+    try {
+      const dataUrl = chartRef.current.toBase64Image('image/png', 1);
+      const link = document.createElement('a');
+      link.href = dataUrl;
+      link.download = exportFilename;
+      document.body.appendChild(link);
+      link.click();
+      document.body.removeChild(link);
+      setExportStatus('exported');
+      if (exportTimerRef.current) {
+        window.clearTimeout(exportTimerRef.current);
+      }
+      exportTimerRef.current = window.setTimeout(() => {
+        setExportStatus('idle');
+      }, 2000);
+    } catch (error) {
+      setExportStatus('idle');
+    }
+  };
+
+  const resolvedExportLabel =
+    exportStatus === 'exporting'
+      ? 'Exporting...'
+      : exportStatus === 'exported'
+        ? 'Exported'
+        : exportLabel;
+
   return (
     <BaseCard
       title={title}
@@ -31,7 +333,17 @@
       icon={<ChartIcon />}
       variant="chart"
       accent
-      theme={theme}
+      theme={resolvedTheme}
+      className={className}
+      actions={
+        <button
+          type="button"
+          onClick={handleExport}
+          className={`agentwp-card__button ${exportStatus === 'exported' ? 'agentwp-card__button--muted' : ''}`}
+        >
+          {resolvedExportLabel}
+        </button>
+      }
     >
       {(metric || trend) && (

+          <ChartComponent
+            id={chartId}
+            ref={chartRef}
+            data={data}
+            options={mergedOptions}
+            plugins={chartPlugins}
+            role="img"
+            aria-describedby={table ? tableId : undefined}
+          />
+        </div>
       </div>
       {footer && <div className="agentwp-card__muted">{footer}</div>}
+      {table && (
+        <div className="agentwp-sr-only">
+          <table id={tableId} className="agentwp-card__table">
+            {table.caption && <caption>{table.caption}</caption>}
+            <thead>
+              <tr>
+                {table.headers.map((header) => (
+                  <th key={header} scope="col">
+                    {header}
+                  </th>
+                ))}
+              </tr>
+            </thead>
+            <tbody>
+              {table.rows.map((row) => (
+                <tr key={row.id}>
+                  {row.cells.map((cell, index) => (
+                    <td key={`${row.id}-${index}`}>{cell}</td>
+                  ))}
+                </tr>
+              ))}
+            </tbody>
+          </table>
+        </div>
+      )}
     </BaseCard>
   );

+const buildDayLabels = (days, prefix = 'Day') =>

+const buildRevenueSeries = (days, base, trend, variance, phase = 0) =>
+  Array.from({ length: days }, (_, index) =>
+    Math.round(base + index * trend + Math.sin(index * 0.45 + phase) * variance)
+  );

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;
+};

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;
+};

+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;

+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;

+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;

+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }

+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };

+            data={data}
+            options={mergedOptions}
+            plugins={chartPlugins}
+            role="img"
+            aria-describedby={table ? tableId : undefined}
+          />
+        </div>
       </div>
       {footer && <div className="agentwp-card__muted">{footer}</div>}
+      {table && (
+        <div className="agentwp-sr-only">
+          <table id={tableId} className="agentwp-card__table">
+            {table.caption && <caption>{table.caption}</caption>}
+            <thead>
+              <tr>
+                {table.headers.map((header) => (
+                  <th key={header} scope="col">
+                    {header}
+                  </th>
+                ))}
+              </tr>
+            </thead>
+            <tbody>
+              {table.rows.map((row) => (
+                <tr key={row.id}>
+                  {row.cells.map((cell, index) => (
+                    <td key={`${row.id}-${index}`}>{cell}</td>
+                  ))}
+                </tr>
+              ))}
+            </tbody>
+          </table>
+        </div>
+      )}
     </BaseCard>
   );
 }

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;

+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;

+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;

+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;

+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }

+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);

   title = 'Performance snapshot',
   subtitle,

+const formatCurrencyValue = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return currencyFormatter.format(value);
+};

+const buildDayLabels = (days, prefix = 'Day') =>
+  Array.from({ length: days }, (_, index) => `${prefix} ${index + 1}`);
+
+const buildRevenueSeries = (days, base, trend, variance, phase = 0) =>
+  Array.from({ length: days }, (_, index) =>
+    Math.round(base + index * trend + Math.sin(index * 0.45 + phase) * variance)
+  );
+
+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;
+};

+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};

+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+

+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;

+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};

+const buildRevenueSeries = (days, base, trend, variance, phase = 0) =>

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;
+};

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};

+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {

+      text: '#0f172a',

+const buildRevenueSeries = (days, base, trend, variance, phase = 0) =>
+  Array.from({ length: days }, (_, index) =>
+    Math.round(base + index * trend + Math.sin(index * 0.45 + phase) * variance)

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;
+};

+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;

+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;

+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;

+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {

+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);

+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};
+
+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {
+  if (theme === 'light') {
+    return {
+      text: '#0f172a',
+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    text: '#e2e8f0',
+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',

+    tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.4)',
+    tooltipText: '#e2e8f0',
+    canvas: '#0b1220',
+  };

   title = 'Performance snapshot',
   subtitle,

+  type = 'line',

+  exportLabel = 'Export PNG',
+  valueFormatter = formatCurrency,
+  yAxisFormatter,
+  className = '',
 }) {
+  const prefersDark = usePrefersDark();
+  const resolvedTheme = theme === 'auto' ? (prefersDark ? 'dark' : 'light') : theme;
+  const palette = useMemo(() => buildChartPalette(resolvedTheme), [resolvedTheme]);
+  const ChartComponent = CHART_COMPONENTS[type] || Line;
+  const chartRef = useRef(null);
+  const exportTimerRef = useRef(null);
+  const [exportStatus, setExportStatus] = useState('idle');
+  const tableId = useId();
+  const chartId = useId();
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    return () => {
+      if (exportTimerRef.current) {
+        window.clearTimeout(exportTimerRef.current);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  const chartPlugins = useMemo(
+    () => [
+      {
+        id: 'agentwpChartBackground',
+        beforeDraw: (chartInstance) => {
+          const { ctx, width, height } = chartInstance;
+          ctx.save();
+          ctx.fillStyle = palette.canvas;
+          ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);
+          ctx.restore();
+        },
+      },
+    ],
+    [palette.canvas]
+  );
+
+  const tooltipCallbacks = useMemo(
+    () => ({
+      label: (context) => {
+        const label = context.dataset?.label ? `${context.dataset.label}: ` : '';
+        const value = resolveTooltipValue(context);
+        return `${label}${valueFormatter(value)}`;
+      },
+    }),
+    [valueFormatter]
+  );
+
+  const mergedOptions = useMemo(() => {
+    const hasScales = type !== 'doughnut';
+    const baseOptions = {
+      responsive: true,
+      maintainAspectRatio: false,
+      devicePixelRatio: 2,
+      animation: {
+        duration: 280,
+        easing: 'easeOutQuart',
+      },
+      interaction: {
+        mode: 'index',
+        intersect: false,
+      },
+      plugins: {
+        legend: {
+          labels: {
+            color: palette.text,
+            font: {
+              family: '"Space Grotesk", "Manrope", system-ui, sans-serif',
+              size: 11,
+              weight: 500,
+            },
+            usePointStyle: true,
+            boxWidth: 8,
+          },
+        },
+        tooltip: {
+          backgroundColor: palette.tooltipBg,
+          borderColor: palette.tooltipBorder,
+          borderWidth: 1,
+          titleColor: palette.tooltipText,
+          bodyColor: palette.tooltipText,
+          callbacks: tooltipCallbacks,
+        },
+      },
+      scales: hasScales

+            x: {
+              ticks: {
+                color: palette.muted,
+              },
+              grid: {
+                color: palette.grid,
+              },
+            },
+            y: {
+              ticks: {
+                color: palette.muted,
+                callback: yAxisFormatter || valueFormatter,
+              },
+              grid: {
+                color: palette.grid,
+              },
+            },
+          }
+        : undefined,
+    };
+
+    if (!options) {

+    return {

+            ...options.plugins?.legend?.labels,
+          },

+        tooltip: {

+    setExportStatus('exporting');
+    try {

+      const link = document.createElement('a');
+      link.href = dataUrl;
+      link.download = exportFilename;
+      document.body.appendChild(link);
+      link.click();
+      document.body.removeChild(link);
+      setExportStatus('exported');
+      if (exportTimerRef.current) {
+        window.clearTimeout(exportTimerRef.current);

+      }, 2000);
+    } catch (error) {
+      setExportStatus('idle');
+    }
+  };
+
+  const resolvedExportLabel =
+    exportStatus === 'exporting'
+      ? 'Exporting...'
+      : exportStatus === 'exported'
+        ? 'Exported'
+        : exportLabel;

+const buildRevenueSeries = (days, base, trend, variance, phase = 0) =>

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;
+};

+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};
+
+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {
+  if (theme === 'light') {
+    return {
+      text: '#0f172a',
+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {

+    muted: '#94a3b8',

+  };

+                {table.headers.map((header) => (
+                  <th key={header} scope="col">
+                    {header}
+                  </th>
+                ))}
+              </tr>
+            </thead>
+            <tbody>
+              {table.rows.map((row) => (
+                <tr key={row.id}>
+                  {row.cells.map((cell, index) => (
+                    <td key={`${row.id}-${index}`}>{cell}</td>
+                  ))}
+                </tr>
+              ))}
+            </tbody>
+          </table>
+        </div>
+      )}
     </BaseCard>
   );
 }

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;

+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {

+  }

+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};

+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',

+  }).format(value);
+};

+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};

+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {

+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;

   title = 'Performance snapshot',
   subtitle,

+  theme = 'auto',
+  type = 'line',

 }) {

+  const resolvedTheme = theme === 'auto' ? (prefersDark ? 'dark' : 'light') : theme;
+  const palette = useMemo(() => buildChartPalette(resolvedTheme), [resolvedTheme]);
+  const ChartComponent = CHART_COMPONENTS[type] || Line;
+  const chartRef = useRef(null);

+  const [exportStatus, setExportStatus] = useState('idle');

+          ctx.save();

+          ctx.fillRect(0, 0, width, height);

+      },

+        : undefined,

+

+        ...options.plugins,
+        legend: {

+          ...options.plugins?.legend,

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {

+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {

+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;

+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;

+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);

+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {

+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;

   title = 'Performance snapshot',

+  theme = 'auto',
+  type = 'line',

+          ctx.restore();
+        },
+      },
+    ],

+  );
+

+    () => ({

+        const label = context.dataset?.label ? `${context.dataset.label}: ` : '';
+        const value = resolveTooltipValue(context);
+        return `${label}${valueFormatter(value)}`;
+      },
+    }),
+    [valueFormatter]

+      maintainAspectRatio: false,
+      devicePixelRatio: 2,
+      animation: {
+        duration: 280,
+        easing: 'easeOutQuart',

+              weight: 500,
+            },
+            usePointStyle: true,
+            boxWidth: 8,
+          },
+        },

+          backgroundColor: palette.tooltipBg,

+                callback: yAxisFormatter || valueFormatter,

+              grid: {
+                color: palette.grid,

+    if (!options) {

+    if (!chartRef.current || exportStatus === 'exporting') {
+      return;
+    }
+    setExportStatus('exporting');
+    try {
+      const dataUrl = chartRef.current.toBase64Image('image/png', 1);
+      const link = document.createElement('a');
+      link.href = dataUrl;
+      link.download = exportFilename;
+      document.body.appendChild(link);
+      link.click();

+      setExportStatus('exported');
+      if (exportTimerRef.current) {
+        window.clearTimeout(exportTimerRef.current);
+      }
+      exportTimerRef.current = window.setTimeout(() => {
+        setExportStatus('idle');
+      }, 2000);
+    } catch (error) {
+      setExportStatus('idle');
+    }
+  };
+
+  const resolvedExportLabel =
+    exportStatus === 'exporting'
+      ? 'Exporting...'
+      : exportStatus === 'exported'
+        ? 'Exported'
+        : exportLabel;
+

+const buildRevenueSeries = (days, base, trend, variance, phase = 0) =>

+    Math.round(base + index * trend + Math.sin(index * 0.45 + phase) * variance)

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;
+};

+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};
+
+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {
+  if (theme === 'light') {
+    return {
+      text: '#0f172a',
+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    text: '#e2e8f0',
+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',
+    tooltipBg: '#0f172a',
+    tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.4)',
+    tooltipText: '#e2e8f0',
+    canvas: '#0b1220',
+  };
+};

 export default function ChartCard({
   title = 'Performance snapshot',
   subtitle,

+  theme = 'auto',

+          ctx.restore();
+        },
+      },
+    ],

+

+        const label = context.dataset?.label ? `${context.dataset.label}: ` : '';
+        const value = resolveTooltipValue(context);
+        return `${label}${valueFormatter(value)}`;
+      },
+    }),
+    [valueFormatter]
+  );
+
+  const mergedOptions = useMemo(() => {
+    const hasScales = type !== 'doughnut';
+    const baseOptions = {
+      responsive: true,
+      maintainAspectRatio: false,
+      devicePixelRatio: 2,
+      animation: {
+        duration: 280,
+        easing: 'easeOutQuart',
+      },
+      interaction: {
+        mode: 'index',
+        intersect: false,
+      },
+      plugins: {
+        legend: {
+          labels: {
+            color: palette.text,
+            font: {
+              family: '"Space Grotesk", "Manrope", system-ui, sans-serif',
+              size: 11,
+              weight: 500,
+            },
+            usePointStyle: true,
+            boxWidth: 8,
+          },
+        },
+        tooltip: {
+          backgroundColor: palette.tooltipBg,
+          borderColor: palette.tooltipBorder,
+          borderWidth: 1,
+          titleColor: palette.tooltipText,
+          bodyColor: palette.tooltipText,
+          callbacks: tooltipCallbacks,
+        },
+      },
+      scales: hasScales
+        ? {
+            x: {
+              ticks: {
+                color: palette.muted,
+              },
+              grid: {
+                color: palette.grid,
+              },
+            },
+            y: {
+              ticks: {
+                color: palette.muted,
+                callback: yAxisFormatter || valueFormatter,
+              },
+              grid: {
+                color: palette.grid,
+              },
+            },
+          }
+        : undefined,
+    };

+    if (!options) {

+      plugins: {

+          ...baseOptions.plugins?.legend,
+          ...options.plugins?.legend,

+            },
+          }

+    if (!chartRef.current || exportStatus === 'exporting') {
+      return;
+    }
+    setExportStatus('exporting');
+    try {
+      const dataUrl = chartRef.current.toBase64Image('image/png', 1);
+      const link = document.createElement('a');
+      link.href = dataUrl;
+      link.download = exportFilename;
+      document.body.appendChild(link);
+      link.click();
+      document.body.removeChild(link);
+      setExportStatus('exported');
+      if (exportTimerRef.current) {
+        window.clearTimeout(exportTimerRef.current);
+      }
+      exportTimerRef.current = window.setTimeout(() => {
+        setExportStatus('idle');
+      }, 2000);
+    } catch (error) {
+      setExportStatus('idle');
+    }
+  };
+
+  const resolvedExportLabel =
+    exportStatus === 'exporting'
+      ? 'Exporting...'
+      : exportStatus === 'exported'
+        ? 'Exported'
+        : exportLabel;
+
   return (
     <BaseCard
       title={title}

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;
+};

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};
+
+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {
+  if (theme === 'light') {
+    return {
+      text: '#0f172a',
+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    text: '#e2e8f0',
+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',
+    tooltipBg: '#0f172a',
+    tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.4)',
+    tooltipText: '#e2e8f0',
+    canvas: '#0b1220',
+  };
+};

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;
+};

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};
+
+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {
+  if (theme === 'light') {
+    return {
+      text: '#0f172a',
+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    text: '#e2e8f0',
+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',
+    tooltipBg: '#0f172a',
+    tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.4)',
+    tooltipText: '#e2e8f0',
+    canvas: '#111827',
+  };
+};

+              </tr>
+            </thead>
+            <tbody>
+              {table.rows.map((row) => (
+                <tr key={row.id}>
+                  {row.cells.map((cell, index) => (
+                    <td key={`${row.id}-${index}`}>{cell}</td>
+                  ))}
+                </tr>
+              ))}
+            </tbody>
+          </table>
+        </div>
+      )}
     </BaseCard>
   );
 }

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {

+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};

+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};

+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {

+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;
+};

+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};
+
+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {
+  if (theme === 'light') {
+    return {
+      text: '#0f172a',
+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    text: '#e2e8f0',
+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',
+    tooltipBg: '#0f172a',
+    tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.4)',
+    tooltipText: '#e2e8f0',
+    canvas: '#111827',
+  };
+};

   title = 'Performance snapshot',

+      },

+      maintainAspectRatio: false,
+      devicePixelRatio: 2,
+      animation: {

+        easing: 'easeOutQuart',

+        mode: 'index',

+              weight: 500,

+            usePointStyle: true,
+            boxWidth: 8,
+          },
+        },
+        tooltip: {

+          bodyColor: palette.tooltipText,

+        },

+            y: {

+                callback: yAxisFormatter || valueFormatter,
+              },
+              grid: {
+                color: palette.grid,
+              },

+      return;

+    setExportStatus('exporting');

+      const link = document.createElement('a');
+      link.href = dataUrl;
+      link.download = exportFilename;
+      document.body.appendChild(link);
+      link.click();

+      setExportStatus('exported');
+      if (exportTimerRef.current) {
+        window.clearTimeout(exportTimerRef.current);
+      }
+      exportTimerRef.current = window.setTimeout(() => {
+        setExportStatus('idle');
+      }, 2000);
+    } catch (error) {
+      setExportStatus('idle');
+    }
+  };
+
+  const resolvedExportLabel =
+    exportStatus === 'exporting'
+      ? 'Exporting...'
+      : exportStatus === 'exported'
+        ? 'Exported'
+        : exportLabel;
+

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;
+};

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};
+
+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {
+  if (theme === 'light') {
+    return {
+      text: '#0f172a',
+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    text: '#e2e8f0',
+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',
+    tooltipBg: '#0f172a',
+    tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.4)',
+    tooltipText: '#e2e8f0',
+    canvas: '#111827',
+  };
+};

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};
+
+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {
+  if (theme === 'light') {
+    return {
+      text: '#0f172a',
+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    text: '#e2e8f0',
+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',
+    tooltipBg: '#0f172a',
+    tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.4)',
+    tooltipText: '#e2e8f0',
+    canvas: '#111827',
+  };
+};
+

   title = 'Performance snapshot',

+        },
+      },

+      },
+    }),
+    [valueFormatter]
+  );
+
+  const mergedOptions = useMemo(() => {
+    const hasScales = type !== 'doughnut';
+    const baseOptions = {
+      responsive: true,
+      maintainAspectRatio: false,
+      devicePixelRatio: 2,
+      animation: {
+        duration: 280,
+        easing: 'easeOutQuart',
+      },
+      interaction: {
+        mode: 'index',
+        intersect: false,
+      },
+      plugins: {
+        legend: {
+          labels: {
+            color: palette.text,

+              weight: 500,
+            },
+            usePointStyle: true,
+            boxWidth: 8,
+          },
+        },
+        tooltip: {
+          backgroundColor: palette.tooltipBg,
+          borderColor: palette.tooltipBorder,
+          borderWidth: 1,
+          titleColor: palette.tooltipText,
+          bodyColor: palette.tooltipText,
+          callbacks: tooltipCallbacks,
+        },
+      },

+            x: {
+              ticks: {

+              },
+              grid: {
+                color: palette.grid,

+            },
+            y: {

+                callback: yAxisFormatter || valueFormatter,

+              grid: {

+              },

+      }, 2000);
+    } catch (error) {
+      setExportStatus('idle');
+    }
+  };
+
+  const resolvedExportLabel =
+    exportStatus === 'exporting'
+      ? 'Exporting...'
+      : exportStatus === 'exported'
+        ? 'Exported'
+        : exportLabel;
+
   return (

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};
+
+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {
+  if (theme === 'light') {
+    return {
+      text: '#0f172a',
+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {

+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',
+    tooltipBg: '#0f172a',

+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);

+  theme = 'auto',

+      },

+        const value = resolveTooltipValue(context);
+        return `${label}${valueFormatter(value)}`;
+      },
+    }),
+    [valueFormatter]
+  );

+  const mergedOptions = useMemo(() => {

+    const baseOptions = {
+      responsive: true,
+      maintainAspectRatio: false,
+      devicePixelRatio: 2,
+      animation: {
+        duration: 280,
+        easing: 'easeOutQuart',

+        mode: 'index',

+              weight: 500,

+            usePointStyle: true,
+            boxWidth: 8,
+          },

+          backgroundColor: palette.tooltipBg,

+                callback: yAxisFormatter || valueFormatter,

+              grid: {
+                color: palette.grid,

+    if (!chartRef.current || exportStatus === 'exporting') {
+      return;
+    }
+    setExportStatus('exporting');
+    try {
+      const dataUrl = chartRef.current.toBase64Image('image/png', 1);
+      const link = document.createElement('a');
+      link.href = dataUrl;
+      link.download = exportFilename;
+      document.body.appendChild(link);
+      link.click();

+      setExportStatus('exported');
+      if (exportTimerRef.current) {
+        window.clearTimeout(exportTimerRef.current);
+      }
+      exportTimerRef.current = window.setTimeout(() => {
+        setExportStatus('idle');
+      }, 2000);
+    } catch (error) {
+      setExportStatus('idle');
+    }
+  };
+
+  const resolvedExportLabel =
+    exportStatus === 'exporting'
+      ? 'Exporting...'
+      : exportStatus === 'exported'
+        ? 'Exported'
+        : exportLabel;
+

       title={title}

+const buildRevenueSeries = (days, base, trend, variance, phase = 0) =>

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;
+};

+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,

+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {

+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    text: '#e2e8f0',
+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',

+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;

+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);

+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};
+
+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {
+  if (theme === 'light') {
+    return {
+      text: '#0f172a',
+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    text: '#e2e8f0',
+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',
+    tooltipBg: '#0f172a',
+    tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.4)',
+    tooltipText: '#e2e8f0',
+    canvas: '#111827',
+  };
+};
+

+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {

+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};

+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;

+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);

+  return prefersDark;

 export default function ChartCard({
   title = 'Performance snapshot',
   subtitle,
   metric,
   trend,
-  chart,
   footer,
-  theme = 'dark',
+  theme = 'auto',
+  type = 'line',
+  data,
+  options,
+  meta,
+  table,
+  height = 220,
+  exportFilename = 'agentwp-chart.png',
+  exportLabel = 'Export PNG',
+  valueFormatter = formatCurrency,
+  yAxisFormatter,
+  className = '',
 }) {
+  const prefersDark = usePrefersDark();
+  const resolvedTheme = theme === 'auto' ? (prefersDark ? 'dark' : 'light') : theme;
+  const palette = useMemo(() => buildChartPalette(resolvedTheme), [resolvedTheme]);
+  const ChartComponent = CHART_COMPONENTS[type] || Line;
+  const chartRef = useRef(null);
+  const exportTimerRef = useRef(null);
+  const [exportStatus, setExportStatus] = useState('idle');
