+          ctx.restore();
+        },
+      },
+    ],
+    [palette.canvas]
+  );
+
+  const tooltipCallbacks = useMemo(
+    () => ({
+      label: (context) => {
+        const label = context.dataset?.label ? `${context.dataset.label}: ` : '';
+        const value = resolveTooltipValue(context);
+        return `${label}${valueFormatter(value)}`;
+      },
+    }),
+    [valueFormatter]
+  );
+
+  const mergedOptions = useMemo(() => {
+    const hasScales = type !== 'doughnut';
+    const baseOptions = {
+      responsive: true,
+      maintainAspectRatio: false,
+      devicePixelRatio: 2,
+      animation: {
+        duration: 280,
+        easing: 'easeOutQuart',
+      },
+      interaction: {
+        mode: 'index',
+        intersect: false,
+      },
+      plugins: {
+        legend: {
+          labels: {
+            color: palette.text,
+            font: {
+              family: '"Space Grotesk", "Manrope", system-ui, sans-serif',
+              size: 11,
+              weight: 500,
+            },
+            usePointStyle: true,
+            boxWidth: 8,
+          },
+        },
+        tooltip: {
+          backgroundColor: palette.tooltipBg,
+          borderColor: palette.tooltipBorder,
+          borderWidth: 1,
+          titleColor: palette.tooltipText,
+          bodyColor: palette.tooltipText,
+          callbacks: tooltipCallbacks,
+        },
+      },
+      scales: hasScales

+            x: {
+              ticks: {
+                color: palette.muted,

+              grid: {
+                color: palette.grid,
+              },
+            },
+            y: {
+              ticks: {
+                color: palette.muted,
+                callback: yAxisFormatter || valueFormatter,
+              },
+              grid: {
+                color: palette.grid,
+              },

+        : undefined,
+    };

+      return baseOptions;

+      ...baseOptions,

+      plugins: {

+        ...options.plugins,
+        legend: {
+          ...baseOptions.plugins?.legend,
+          ...options.plugins?.legend,

+            ...options.plugins?.legend?.labels,
+          },

+        tooltip: {
+          ...baseOptions.plugins?.tooltip,

+    if (!chartRef.current || exportStatus === 'exporting') {
+      return;
+    }
+    setExportStatus('exporting');
+    try {
+      const dataUrl = chartRef.current.toBase64Image('image/png', 1);
+      const link = document.createElement('a');
+      link.href = dataUrl;
+      link.download = exportFilename;
+      document.body.appendChild(link);
+      link.click();
+      document.body.removeChild(link);
+      setExportStatus('exported');
+      if (exportTimerRef.current) {
+        window.clearTimeout(exportTimerRef.current);
+      }
+      exportTimerRef.current = window.setTimeout(() => {
+        setExportStatus('idle');
+      }, 2000);
+    } catch (error) {
+      setExportStatus('idle');
+    }
+  };
+
+  const resolvedExportLabel =
+    exportStatus === 'exporting'
+      ? 'Exporting...'
+      : exportStatus === 'exported'
+        ? 'Exported'
+        : exportLabel;
+
   return (
     <BaseCard
       title={title}

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;
+};

+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};
+
+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+    style: 'currency',
+    currency: 'USD',
+    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+  }).format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {
+  if (theme === 'light') {
+    return {
+      text: '#0f172a',
+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    text: '#e2e8f0',
+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',
+    tooltipBg: '#0f172a',
+    tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.4)',
+    tooltipText: '#e2e8f0',
+    canvas: '#111827',
+  };
+};

+      document.body.appendChild(link);

+    } catch (error) {

+    }
+  };
+
+  const resolvedExportLabel =
+    exportStatus === 'exporting'
+      ? 'Exporting...'
+      : exportStatus === 'exported'
+        ? 'Exported'
+        : exportLabel;

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;

**Optimizing ChartCard formatting function**

I'm checking that ChartCard correctly uses `chartId` and passes the `actions` prop as expected. I’m also reviewing `valueFormatter` usage within memoized hooks to ensure dependencies are accurate. Noticing that `formatCurrency` creates a new `Intl.NumberFormat` on every call, I want to optimize performance by moving that formatter outside the function to reuse it efficiently. This small tweak should help with rendering speed without breaking existing behavior.

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {
+  line: Line,
+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,
+};
+
+const currencyFormatter = new Intl.NumberFormat('en-US', {
+  style: 'currency',
+  currency: 'USD',
+  maximumFractionDigits: 0,
+});
+
+const formatCurrency = (value) => {
+  if (typeof value !== 'number' || Number.isNaN(value)) {
+    return value?.toString() ?? '';
+  }
+  return currencyFormatter.format(value);
+};
+
+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};
+
+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
+
+const buildChartPalette = (theme) => {
+  if (theme === 'light') {
+    return {
+      text: '#0f172a',
+      muted: '#475569',
+      grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.35)',
+      tooltipBg: '#ffffff',
+      tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.6)',
+      tooltipText: '#0f172a',
+      canvas: '#f1f5f9',
+    };
+  }
+  return {
+    text: '#e2e8f0',
+    muted: '#94a3b8',
+    grid: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.2)',
+    tooltipBg: '#0f172a',
+    tooltipBorder: 'rgba(148, 163, 184, 0.4)',
+    tooltipText: '#e2e8f0',
+    canvas: '#111827',
+  };
+};

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {

+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;

+const CHART_COMPONENTS = {

+  bar: Bar,
+  doughnut: Doughnut,

+  }
+  return currencyFormatter.format(value);
+};

+const resolveTooltipValue = (context) => {
+  if (typeof context.parsed === 'number') {
+    return context.parsed;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.y !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.y;
+  }
+  if (context.parsed?.r !== undefined) {
+    return context.parsed.r;
+  }
+  return context.raw;
+};

+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });

+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;

+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);

+  return prefersDark;
+};

+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {

+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;

+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};

+  theme = 'auto',

+      },

+      },
+    }),

+  );

+      maintainAspectRatio: false,

+      animation: {
+        duration: 280,

+        mode: 'index',

+              weight: 500,

+            usePointStyle: true,
+            boxWidth: 8,
+          },

+          backgroundColor: palette.tooltipBg,

+            },
+            y: {

+                color: palette.muted,
+                callback: yAxisFormatter || valueFormatter,
+              },
+              grid: {
+                color: palette.grid,
+              },

+      return;
+    }
+    setExportStatus('exporting');
+    try {

+      const link = document.createElement('a');
+      link.href = dataUrl;
+      link.download = exportFilename;
+      document.body.appendChild(link);
+      link.click();

+      setExportStatus('exported');
+      if (exportTimerRef.current) {
+        window.clearTimeout(exportTimerRef.current);
+      }
+      exportTimerRef.current = window.setTimeout(() => {
+        setExportStatus('idle');
+      }, 2000);
+    } catch (error) {
+      setExportStatus('idle');
+    }
+  };
+
+  const resolvedExportLabel =
+    exportStatus === 'exporting'
+      ? 'Exporting...'
+      : exportStatus === 'exported'
+        ? 'Exported'
+        : exportLabel;
+
   return (
     <BaseCard
       title={title}

     </BaseCard>

+const hexToRgba = (hex, alpha) => {
+  const cleanHex = hex.replace('#', '');
+  if (cleanHex.length !== 6) {
+    return hex;
+  }
+  const r = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(0, 2), 16);
+  const g = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(2, 4), 16);
+  const b = parseInt(cleanHex.slice(4, 6), 16);
+  return `rgba(${r}, ${g}, ${b}, ${alpha})`;
+};

+const usePrefersDark = (fallback = true) => {
+  const [prefersDark, setPrefersDark] = useState(() => {
+    if (typeof window === 'undefined' || !window.matchMedia) {
+      return fallback;
+    }
+    return window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
+  });
+
+  useEffect(() => {
+    if (!window.matchMedia) {
+      return undefined;
+    }
+    const media = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
+    const handleChange = (event) => {
+      setPrefersDark(event.matches);
+    };
+    if (media.addEventListener) {
+      media.addEventListener('change', handleChange);
+    } else {
+      media.addListener(handleChange);
+    }
+    return () => {
+      if (media.removeEventListener) {
+        media.removeEventListener('change', handleChange);
+      } else {
+        media.removeListener(handleChange);
+      }
+    };
+  }, []);
+
+  return prefersDark;
+};
